# 3.14 Radio Network Temporary Identifier management

## 3.14.0-4 Radio Network Temporary Identifier management (Temporary) C-RNTI Generator (ID: 11151993)

**3.14.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11151999`)

Radio Network Temporary Identifier management
Refer to

5G\_UP\_ALG\_3394\_replaced([11152003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Allocation of a C-RNTI

5G\_UP\_ALG\_3399\_replaced([11152029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmJfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Creation of the list of free C-RNTI

5G\_UP\_ALG\_3403\_replaced([11152041](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Generation of a pool of C-RNTI

---

## 3.14.0-5 Radio Network Temporary Identifier management Allocation of a C-RNTI (ID: 11152003)

**3.14.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11152024`)

Radio Network Temporary Identifier management
In this requirement and in the requirements referred from this requirement, C-RNTI shall refer to any of:

- (temporary) C-RNTI for RA procedure

- CS-RNTI for uplink configured grant

5G-L2-PS shall generate a (temporary) C-RNTI whenever needed, e.g. when creating a temporary UE context upon reception of a RA preamble or when UE setup without C-RNTI.

A C-RNTI value is allocated by taking (and removing) the first one from the list of free C-RNTIs.

If the cell as SCell is FR1 cell and C-RNTI belong to its (SCell) C-RNTI pool during CA UE SCell addition:

Then:

5G-L2-PS SCell shall remove C-RNTI from a pool till release CA UE.

A C-RNTI value is released by putting it back to the end of the list of free C-RNTIs.

Independent of which subcell is UE’s Pcell, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate a C-RNTI from the pool of available values. That means a single C-RNTI is assigned to only one UE. Please note that the same C-RNTI is used on all carriers of a CA UE.

If the cell is FR1 cell:

For FDD cell with one non-overlapping pool and one overlapping pool, gNB-DU shall make sure the C-RNTI allocated from overlapping range is not used until C-RNTI from non-overlapping range is used up. gNB-DU need make sure the freed C-RNTIs are not re-used immediately.

If the cell as SCell is FR1 cell, during CA UE SCell addition procedure, 5G-L2-PS of SCell no need to check whether the allocated C-RNTI which the UE's PCell belongs to its own non-overlapping pool or not.

Note:

For FDD cell, CP-RT may indicate one non-overlapping pool and one overlapping pool or two pools in non-overlapped [PR763713] or two non-overlapping pool and one overlapping pool[End PR763713], L2-PS need to follow the C-RNTI range granted by CPRT. Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For FR1 TDD cell, control plane will provide two or four pool indexes in non-overlapping range.

The CRNTI pool allocation concept is defined according to 5G\_CP\_OTH\_267\_replaced([11597181](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y23Z7PwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

## 3.14.0-6 Radio Network Temporary Identifier management Creation of the list of free C-RNTI (ID: 11152029)

**3.14.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11152035`)

Radio Network Temporary Identifier management
The range of the 16-bit wide C-RNTI shall be 0x1 to 0xFFEF.

if the cell is FR2 cell,

The range of C-RNTI values is shared among the cells with same crntiPoolId as follows and managed by a DL/UL scheduler couple [5G\_UP\_7320\_replaced([11386856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufEDdPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]. Note: even if no CA, each crntiPoolId as a unique list of CRNTI because of 5G-L2-LO searching a user context only on CRNTI criteria.

if the cell is FR1 cell,

The total range of the 16-bit wide C-RNTI are divided into three parts: a. Dedicated range for RA-RNTI, b. non-overlapping range, c. overlapping range.

Control plane will provide the starting point of overlapping part with the smallest CRNTI value in overlapping part.

a. 0x1 to 0x12C are dedicated for RA-RNTI which can be used for all cells.

Note-1: once the range of RA-RNTI is changed for FR1 TDD and FDD cells, the algorithm need be re-designed.

b. 0x12D to Smallest CRNTI value in overlapping part-1 are for non-overlapping range.

c. Smallest CRNTI value in overlapping part to 0xFFEF are for overlapping range.

For C-RNTI pool management and allocation, please refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The values for RA-RNTI shall be filtered out as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3412\_replaced([11152133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

One extra C-RNTI shall be created according to the algorithm above and be used exclusively for the purposes of artificial PDSCH load and shall not be included in the list of free C-RNTIs. The decreased Hamming distance is not harmful, because artificial PDSCH load does not create a DCI. Filtering for RA-RNTI does not apply to C-RNTI for artificial PDSCH load

---

## 3.14.1 Generation of a pool of C-RNTI

### 3.14.1.0-1 Generation of a pool of C-RNTI Generation of a pool of C-RNTI for FR1 Cell (ID: 11152046)

**3.14.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11152052`)

Generation of a pool of C-RNTI
For FR1 FDD cell, the CRNTI table is combined with one non-overlapping pool and one overlapping pool or two non-overlapping pool which is controlled by CP-RT. Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For FR1 TDD cell, the CRNTI table is combined with 2 non-overlapping pool or 4 non-overlapping pool which is controlled by CP-RT, Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

One extra C-RNTI shall be reserved and be used exclusively for the purposes of artificial PDSCH load and shall not be included in the list of free C-RNTIs.  For simple handling, the last CRNTI in the final table of each cell is reserved for it.

That means the last CRNTI in the last overlapping table if cell is granted with one non-overlapping table and one overlapping table or last non-overlapping table if cell is granted with non-overlapping table only.

L2-PS should derive CRNTI table from non-overlapping pool and one overlapping pool refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9024\_replaced([11152073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.14.1.0-2 Generation of a pool of C-RNTI Generation of a pool of C-RNTI For FR2 Cell (ID: 11152058)

**3.14.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11152068`)

Generation of a pool of C-RNTI
If the cell is FR2 cell, upon setup of the first cell with a new value of crntiPoolId, corresponding DL/UL scheduler couple shall have its own free CRNTI table. First C-RNTI value calculated as follows:

p(0) = (61 + crntiPoolId \* Coef) mod 65536

where

* crntiPoolId is C-RNTI pool ID, defined in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Coef is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3408\_replaced([11152150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Any further value shall be derived from the previously calculated value by applying the following formula until maximum values of different CRNTI values has been reached (see below):

p(n) = (p(n-1) + maxNbOfCRNTIPools \* Coef) mod 65536

with

* maxNbOfCRNTIPools is the number of C-RNTI pools, defined 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Coef is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3408\_replaced([11152150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The minimum Hamming distance between the C-RNTI values (in cells handled by a 5G-L2-PS instance) shall be depending on Coef used and maximum number of CRNTI needed (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3408\_replaced([11152150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3408\_replaced([11152150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to see different number of C-RNTI having minimum hamming distance of 3 or 2 depending on Coef value used and maximum number of CRNTI needed.

[CNI-88099-M] [End CNI-88099-M]

---

## 3.14.2 C-RNTI table derivation

## 3.14.2-1 C-RNTI table derivation

**3.14.2-1.0-2**  (ID: `11152144`)

C-RNTI table derivation
For each NRCELL at cell setup, 5G-L2-PS shall filter out the RA-RNTI values from the list of free C-RNTI values. This shall be done once the cell is configured using following logic:

1. L2 PS shall compute all the potential “PRACH occasion” based on prach-ConfigIndex (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1961\_replaced([11111920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRIPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and association between prach-ConfigIndex and  transmitted SS block (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1970\_replaced([11111961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRvS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[Before CB008474-A]

1. For any potential PRACH occasion, L2 PS shall compute the s\_id, t\_id, f\_id as
2. s\_id is the index of the first OFDM symbol of the specified PRACH (0≤ s\_id< 14) (refers to 3GPP 38321 chapter5.1.3). I.e. L2-PS shall set the values s\_id to:

s\_id = prachStartSymbol + rrmPreambleOccasionLength\_symbols\*prachPreambleTimeOccasion,

where prachStartSymbol and rrmPreambleOccasionLength\_symbols is defined according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1959\_replaced([11111903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRIOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* f\_id is the index of the specified PRACH occasion within the slot in the frequency domain (0≤ f\_id< 8). Only 1 PRACH occasion in the frequency domain and hence only 1 f\_id value shall be supported. L2-PS shall set the value of f\_id to:

f\_id = 0.

Note: The number of supported PRACH occasions in the frequency domain corresponds to IE msg1-FDM in 38.311.

* t\_id is the index of the first slot of the specified PRACH (0≤ t\_id< X). The value of X is determined by the SCS, i.e. subcarrier spacing, e.g., 0≤ t\_id <20 for 30kHz SCS, 0≤ t\_id <40 for 60kHz SCS, and 0≤ t\_id <80 for 120kHz SCS. I.e. L2-PS shall set the values of t\_id to:

t\_id = X - p2,

where the values of p2 are p2 = [1, 2] for 30kHz SCS and p2 = [23, 22, 21, 3, 2, 1] for 120kHz SCS, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1961\_replaced([11111920](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRIPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The case with 60kHz SCS is not implemented currently

For FDD cell while actInterNumerologyCa is true according to 5G\_UP\_1278\_replaced([11357256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucbmN_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), s\_id is set as 14, t\_id is set as 20 and f\_id is set as 0.

[End CB008474-A]

1. L2 PS shall filter out any RNTI values from the list of free CRNTI values corresponding to:

RA-RNTI = 1 + s\_id + 14*(t\_id + 80*f\_id), with RA-RNTI formula is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3384\_replaced([11152563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgpffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

for FDD, RA-RNTI is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3385\_replaced([11152543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgpevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

for TDD FR1 long preamble format, RA-RNTI is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3385\_replaced([11152543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgpevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008474-A]

for TDD FR1 short preamble format, RA-RNTI is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3384\_replaced([11152563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksgpffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008474-A]

Notes: The aim of this extra logic is to avoid to reserve the first 8960 ( = 14*80*8) CRNTI  to the RA-RNTI. Once the prach-ConfigIndex is specified by 3GPP, it shall be evaluated whether the number of CRNTI is large enough to support the targeted UE capacity.

if the cell is FR1 cell,

the CRNTI is allocated in static way and the RA-CRNTI is excluded for all FR1 TDD cells and FDD cells.

The first 300 CRNTIs, not 8960 CRNTIs based on 5G21B and 22R1 requiremens, are dedicated for RA-RNTI for FR1 TDD cell and FDD cell based on

RA-RNTI = 1 + s\_id + 14*(t\_id + 80*f\_id)

S\_id is set as 14, t\_id is set as 20 and f\_id is set as 0.

For FDD cell while actInterNumerologyCa is true according to 5G\_UP\_1278\_replaced([11357256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucbmN_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), s\_id is set as 14, t\_id is set as 20 and f\_id is set as 0.

Note-1: once the range of RA-RNTI is changed for FR1 TDD and FDD cells, the algorithm used by 5GC002546 need be re-designed.

---

## 3.14.2-2 C-RNTI table derivation

**3.14.2-2.0-2**  (ID: `11152174`)

C-RNTI table derivation
11152174:
C-RNTI table derivation
To handle high increase of CRNTI number, different Coef value shall be used depending of maximum capacity required. There may also be a need depending of maximum capacity required to include CRNTI with minimum hamming distance of 2 or 1 between them.
 
if the cell is FR2 cell,
 
There are still one CRNTI pool per crntiPoolId and each CRNTI in one crntiPoolId is unique.
 
With formula in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3391\_replaced([11151993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksc_HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) first computed CRNTI have a minimum hamming distance of 3 between them. When maximum of CRNTI with minimum hamming distance of 3 is reached, next computed CRNTIs will have a minimum hamming distance of 2 between them. Its same when maximum of CRNTI with minimum hamming distance of 2 is reached, next computed CRNTIs will have a minimum hamming distance of 1 between them.
 
Table 1 below gives maximum number of CRNTI having a minimum hamming distance of 3 (MHD3) and 2 (MHD2) depending of Coef used (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3391\_replaced([11151993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksc_HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for formula details). It indicates also feature impacts. Note: Several features are marked by TBD. It shall be filled by indicated feature CFAM.
 
Table 1 legend:
      Coef: Coefficient used in formula in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3391\_replaced([11151993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksc_HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
      HDx: maximum number of CRNTI having minimum hamming distance “x” between them.
      maxNbOfCRNTIPools : maximum number of C-RNTI pool to be supported
 
| | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Coef | MHD3 | MHD2 | Functional requirement per feature |
| 39887 | 581 | 4096 | Not used |
| 37 | 1770 | 5313 | Used for all maxNbOfCRNTIPools values. Only CRNTI with MHD3 used. [Before CNI-103796-M] vDU specific: Used for all maxNbOfCRNTIPools values. [End CNI-103796-M] |
| 67 | 979 | 6845 | Not used |
| 27749 | 591 | 9728 | Coef = 27749 and Pool with MHD2 is used if long PUCCH is configured to support up to 1120 UEs per FDD or FR1 TDD cell while maxNbOfCRNTIPools = 6 when actInterNumerologyCa = true according to 5G\_UP\_1278\_replaced([11357256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucbmN_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). |
Table 1.
 
Table 2 below gives CRNTI capacity depending of release, feature, maxNbOfCRNTIPools and indicates which COEF shall be used. Please note that COEF is selected in a way that number of CRNTI in HD3 is as maximum as possible. A marge of 16% on number of CRNTI is added to handled CRNTI timer release and issue with RRC release procedure.

### 3.14.2.0-1 C-RNTI table derivation C-RNTI table derivation for non-overlapped part (ID: 11152079)

**3.14.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11152085`)

C-RNTI table derivation
Input:

crntiNonOverlappingPoolId[];

crntiOverlappingStart;

maxNbOfCRNTIPools; maxNbOfCRNTIPools is the number of C-RNTI pools, defined 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

notes:

maxNbOfCRNTIPools

The number of Crnti Pools.

Functional specification in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3391\_replaced([11151993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksc_HPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Before CB007737, it fixed as 72 pools for FR1 cell.

If NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption is set to 144 with maxNbOfCRNTIPools equals to 144, else NRBTS/NRDU/CrntiAllocationOption is set to 72 with maxNbOfCRNTIPools equals to 72 for FR1 cells.

Algorithm:

Non-overlapping CRNTI table calculation for first pool (common for FR1 FDD and FR1 TDD cell):

First C-RNTI value calculated as follows based on crntiNonOverLappingPoolId [0]:

p(0) = (61 + crntiNonOverlappingPoolId [0] \* Coef) mod 65536

where

* crntiNonOverlappingPoolId[0] the Pool ID of non-overlaping CRNTI blocks (refer to 5G\_CP\_OTH\_267\_replaced([11597181](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y23Z7PwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* Coef is harcoded as 27749.

Any further value shall be derived from the previously calculated value by applying the following formula until maximum values of different CRNTI values has been reached (see below):

p(n) = (p(n-1) + maxNbOfCRNTIPools \* Coef) mod 65536

with

* maxNbOfCRNTIPools is delivered from CP-RT which is the max number of cells in one DU;
* Coef is harcoded as 27749.

Maximum values of different CRNTI values is derived based on maxNbOfCRNTIPools, then nmax < (0xFFEF+1)/ maxNbOfCRNTIPools, 0xFFEF is max available CRNTI defined in 3GPP R15.

Then filter out RA-RNTI and overlapping range from the list, to make sure p(i) in (RA-RANTI max, crntiOverlappingStart). Max RA-RNTI is refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3412\_replaced([11152133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kseNN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Non-overlapping range calculation for other non-overlapping pool is the same algorithm as applied with first non-overlapping pool

---

### 3.14.2.0-2 C-RNTI table derivation C-RNTI table derived for overlapped part (ID: 11152092)

**3.14.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11152097`)

C-RNTI table derivation
Input:

crntiOverlappingStart;

crntiOverlappingPoolId;

maxNbOfCRNTIPools; maxNbOfCRNTIPools is the number of C-RNTI pools, defined 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool; if maxNbOfCRNTIPools is equal to 72, the value is set to 6, else the value is set  to 1.

Algorithm:

Overlapping CRNTI table calculation

for FDD:

Another round of CRNTI allocation is needed for cells granted with overlapping pool to get the CRNTIs from overlapping range.

The total CRNTI numbers in overlapping range is:

* totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI = 0xFFEF – overlappingCRNTIStart +1, overlappingCRNTIStart is start CRNTI of overlaping CRNTI blocks (refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2067\_replaced([11278563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpQ_WPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI is divided by nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool, the remainder need be taken from totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI.
* nbOfOverlappingCRNTIPerPool = totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI/nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool
* totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI = nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool\*nbOfOverlappingCRNTIPerPool

C-RNTI table per overlapping pool is calculated as follows:

p(0) = (61 + crntiOverlappingPoolId \* Coef) mod totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI

where

* crntiOverlappingPoolId is the Pool ID of overlaping CRNTI blocks (refer to 5G\_CP\_OTH\_267\_replaced([11597181](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y23Z7PwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* Coef is hardcoded as 37;
* nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool is 6 which is the max number of FDD cells in one L2RT instance

Any further value shall be derived from the previously calculated value by applying the following formula until maximum values of different CRNTI values has been reached (see below):

p(n) = (p(n-1) + nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool\* Coef) mod totalNumbOfOverlappingCRNTI

with

* nbOfCRNTIOverlappingPool if maxNbOfCRNTIPools is equal to 72, the value is set to 6, else the value is set  to 1.
* Coef is hardcoded as 37;
* n < nbOfOverlappingCRNTIPerPool;

Note-3: if the max number of FDD cells in one L2RT instance is changed, the algorithm need be re-designed.

Then C-RNTI table in overlapping pool is:

p(i) = p(i)+ overlappingCRNTIStart, i=0,n-1.

---

### 3.14.2.0-3 C-RNTI table derivation C-RNTI table derivation example (ID: 11152104)
